class="wp-block-media-text__content"> <div style="height:1px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div> <p class="gb-headline gb-headline-84411404 gb-headline-text">Seniors deserve the freedom to live their best lives!</p> <p class="has-medium-font-size">We (Dayna &amp; Ben) created loaids.com to provide advice on strategies and tools to assist in raising your levels of independence and happiness.</p> <p class="has-medium-font-size">We believe that Helping Older People increase their independence is the best way of achieving their Freedom.</p> <p class="has-medium-font-size">Whether it’s Travel, Friendship, Adventure, or Fitness, we know that Seniors’ care can be enhanced through mindset, exercise, participation and the use of mobility equipment and daily living aids.</p> <p>So Wheelchair Ramps for Vans?, Yoga for the Elderly? or Nintendo Switch for Seniors? – We’ve done the homework for you!</p> </div></div> <div style="height:43px" aria-hidden="true" passionate about seniors’ care and well-being.
